class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column14_76852b-b2"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-a3e41b62850a08c33f1c12ccfc645532"><strong>Meta Kuwait Portal Registration Process</strong></h2></div></div></div></div><p></p><p class="has-black-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-5ab40867723e9fc7e02c0e074f611384">Meta Kuwait Portal is free to use. To access Meta Kuwait Portal&#8217;s services, Kuwaiti residents must register as new users. Registration and login for <strong>Meta Kuwait</strong> require a <a href="https://kuwaitcivilidchecks.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Civil ID</a>. Login is required to access Meta Portal Services.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Step 1: Visit the Meta Kuwait website</strong></h3><p></p><div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img data-lazyloaded="1" src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIHdpZHRoPSIxMDI0IiBoZWlnaHQ9IjQ0MCIgdmlld0JveD0iMCAwIDEwMjQgNDQwIj48cmVjdCB3aWR0aD0iMTAwJSIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxMDAlIiBzdHlsZT0iZmlsbDojY2ZkNGRiO2ZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eTogMC4xOyIvPjwvc3ZnPg==" decoding="async" width="1024" height="440" data-src="https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/image-1024x440.png.webp" alt="" class="wp-image-15" style="width:862px;height:auto" data-srcset="https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/image-1024x440.png.webp 1024w, https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/image-1024x440.png-300x129.webp 300w, https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/image-1024x440.png-768x330.webp 768w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></figure></div><p></p><p>You can register yourself as a new user at <a href="https://metaprodapp.azurewebsites.net/En/Account/Login?ReturnUrl=%2FEn%2FHome%2FIndex" target="_blank" rel="noopener">metaprodapp.azurewebsites.net</a>. Clicking on the given link will take you to the Meta Portal homepage.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Step 2: Click on Register as a New User</strong></h3><p></p><div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img data-lazyloaded="1" src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIHdpZHRoPSI2NjMiIGhlaWdodD0iNjE0IiB2aWV3Qm94PSIwIDAgNjYzIDYxNCI+PHJlY3Qgd2lkdGg9IjEwMCUiIGhlaWdodD0iMTAwJSIgc3R5bGU9ImZpbGw6I2NmZDRkYjtmaWxsLW9wYWNpdHk6IDAuMTsiLz48L3N2Zz4=" loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="663" height="614" data-src="https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/Capture.png" alt="" class="wp-image-16" style="width:520px;height:auto" data-srcset="https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/Capture.png 663w, https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/Capture-300x278.png 300w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 663px) 100vw, 663px" /></figure></div><p></p><p>Meta Kuwait Portal shows a login screen on the left and instructions on the right. On the registration page, you should find the &#8220;<strong>Register As a New User</strong>&#8221; option.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Step 3: Fill in the Personal Information</strong></h3><p></p><div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img data-lazyloaded="1" src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIHdpZHRoPSIxMDI0IiBoZWlnaHQ9IjMyNyIgdmlld0JveD0iMCAwIDEwMjQgMzI3Ij48cmVjdCB3aWR0aD0iMTAwJSIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxMDAlIiBzdHlsZT0iZmlsbDojY2ZkNGRiO2ZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eTogMC4xOyIvPjwvc3ZnPg==" loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="327" data-src="https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/cc.png" alt="" class="wp-image-17" style="width:860px;height:auto" data-srcset="https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/cc.png 1024w, https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/cc-300x96.png 300w, https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/cc-768x245.png 768w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></figure></div><p></p><p>Now you must enter four important details about yourself. Enter your Civil ID Number first, then your Civil ID Serial Number. Enter your mobile number and email address next. Enter all the information correctly.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Step 4: Accept the Terms &amp; Conditions</strong></h3><p></p><div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large is-resized"><img data-lazyloaded="1" src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIHdpZHRoPSIxMDI0IiBoZWlnaHQ9IjgxIiB2aWV3Qm94PSIwIDAgMTAyNCA4MSI+PHJlY3Qgd2lkdGg9IjEwMCUiIGhlaWdodD0iMTAwJSIgc3R5bGU9ImZpbGw6I2NmZDRkYjtmaWxsLW9wYWNpdHk6IDAuMTsiLz48L3N2Zz4=" loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="81" data-src="https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/Capture-1-1024x81.png" alt="" class="wp-image-18" style="width:947px;height:auto" data-srcset="https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/Capture-1-1024x81.png 1024w, https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/Capture-1-300x24.png 300w, https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/Capture-1-768x61.png 768w, https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/Capture-1-1536x122.png 1536w, https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/Capture-1.png 1871w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></figure></div><p></p><p>Read the Terms and Conditions link carefully. After that, tick the box to accept the Meta Kuwait Portal&#8217;s terms and conditions.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Step 5: Click on the Register button</strong></h3><p></p><div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img data-lazyloaded="1" src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIHdpZHRoPSIxMDI0IiBoZWlnaHQ9IjMyNyIgdmlld0JveD0iMCAwIDEwMjQgMzI3Ij48cmVjdCB3aWR0aD0iMTAwJSIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxMDAlIiBzdHlsZT0iZmlsbDojY2ZkNGRiO2ZpbGwtb3BhY2l0eTogMC4xOyIvPjwvc3ZnPg==" loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="327" data-src="https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/cc-1.png" alt="" class="wp-image-20" style="width:866px;height:auto" data-srcset="https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/cc-1.png 1024w, https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/cc-1-300x96.png 300w, https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/cc-1-768x245.png 768w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></figure></div><p></p><p>To register yourself at the Meta Kuwait Portal, click on Register.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading">Step 6: Get Your Meta Kuwait Account Activated</h3><p>A new email has been sent to you from the Meta Portal. Biometric Registration</h2></div></div></div></div><p></p><p>Kuwait and the GCC countries require all citizens and residents to register their biometrics. Click on the Biometric Enrollment Service link at the bottom to schedule an appointment.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading">Step 7: Choose a Biometric Appointment Date &amp; Time</h3><p></p><div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img data-lazyloaded="1" src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIHdpZHRoPSI3NjgiIGhlaWdodD0iNDMwIiB2aWV3Qm94PSIwIDAgNzY4IDQzMCI+PHJlY3Qgd2lkdGg9IjEwMCUiIGhlaWdodD0iMTAwJSIgc3R5bGU9ImZpbGw6I2NmZDRkYjtmaWxsLW9wYWNpdHk6IDAuMTsiLz48L3N2Zz4=" loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="768" height="430" data-src="https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/gdfs.png" alt="" class="wp-image-30" style="width:829px;height:auto" data-srcset="https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/gdfs.png 768w, https://metaportalhelp.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/gdfs-300x168.png 300w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px" /></figure></div><p></p><p>Finally, you should choose your desired date and time for your biometric appointment at the office of the General Department of Personnel Identification.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading">Step 8: Confirm the appointment and verify your details</h3><p></p><p>Schedule a time and date to register/update your biometrics. Your appointment will be confirmed once you verify your details and click on submit.</p><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id14_7a75f6-7a alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top"><div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column14_8a138b-5d"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="has-text-align-center">You Must Read: <a href="https://metaportalhelp.com/meta-portal-appointment-for-civil-id-address-change/"><strong>Meta Portal Appointment for Civil ID Address Change</strong></a></p></div></div></div></div><p></p><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id14_9ab8b7-4b alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top"><div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column14_3e0bf9-75"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-6568fb7ca85b2bb9d9684183ffb4cdd4"><strong>Meta Portal Appointment For Civil ID</strong></h2></div></div></div></div><p></p><p>The process of booking a Civil ID appointment through Kuwait&#8217;s Meta Portal is straightforward. You can do this by following these steps:</p><ul class="wp-block-list"><li>Visit the <strong>&#8220;Appointments&#8221; </strong>section after logging in.</li><li>Choose <strong>&#8220;Public Authority for Civil Information.&#8221;</strong></li><li>Select your service<strong>, date, and time.</strong></li><li>Please<strong> review </strong>and<strong> submit </strong>your request<strong>.</strong></li></ul><p></p><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id14_2797f7-35 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top"><div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column14_05657a-3f"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-9c1e5e33324ca4c5f4715a87d22a0b51"><strong>Meta Portal Biometric Appointment</strong></h2></div></div></div></div><p></p><p><strong>Here are the steps you need to take to schedule a biometric appointment on Meta Kuwait:</strong></p><ul class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Step 1. </strong>Visit the<strong> Meta portal.</strong></li><li><strong>Step 2. </strong>Select<strong> &#8220;Appointments&#8221; by clicking the <strong>Services icon</strong> under the appropriate management.</li><li><strong>Step 10:</strong> Click the Apply icon for the <strong>service you wish</strong> to schedule.</li><li><strong>Step 11:</strong> Choose the branch where the service will be provided by clicking the respective<strong> Apply</strong> button.</li><li><strong>Step 12:</strong> Select your preferred<strong> date and time</strong>, then <strong>confirm your new appointment</strong>.</li></ul><p>By following these steps, you can easily modify your appointment on the Meta Kuwait platform.</p><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id14_434f39-ad alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit An individual can book an appointment with any government office/department through the portal.</p><p>The service employee is also available by video call (conference call) for people living in remote areas.</p><p></p><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id14_dd1c15-e2 alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top"><div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column14_b22bbb-17"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-1611d723f2bc1cca3fe96a383aa52a77">Meta Kuwait&nbsp;Civil ID Already Registered</h2></div></div></div></div><p></p><p>If you see the error <strong>&#8220;Civil ID Already Registered&#8221;</strong> on Meta Kuwait, it means your Civil ID number is already linked to another account. Follow these steps to resolve the issue:</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Check for an Existing Account</strong></h3><p>If you’ve created an account before, try logging in with your previous credentials. Use the &#8220;Forgot Password&#8221; option to reset your password if needed.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Contact Meta Kuwait Support</strong></h3><ul class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Email</strong>: Send an email to Meta Kuwait support and attach your Civil ID for verification.</li><li><strong>Call</strong>: Reach out to their customer service helpline for assistance.</li></ul><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Update Your Details</strong></h3><p>If there’s an error with your Civil ID details, request Meta Kuwait to update your information.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Report Fraud</strong></h3><p>If you believe someone else has used your Civil ID, file a formal complaint with Meta Kuwait and provide proof of ownership of the Civil ID.</p><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id14_d0f262-c9 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top"><div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column14_5e58bb-38"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><p class="has-text-align-center">You Must Read: <strong><a href="https://metaportalhelp.com/meta-kuwait-login-password-issues/">Meta Kuwait Login Password Issues</a></strong></p></div></div></div></div><p></p><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id14_d312f8-bd alignnone kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top"><div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column14_6bedb3-df"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-2c7ea9297237dd481f22fd87a327b1e6">Benefits of Meta Kuwait</h2></div></div></div></div><p></p><p>The Meta Kuwait Portal is a game-changer for individuals and organizations. Here’s why:</p><figure class="wp-block-table"><table><thead><tr><th>Benefits</th><th>Details</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><strong>Time-Saving</strong></td><td>No more waiting in long queues; access class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>What is Meta in Kuwait?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner"><p>Meta is a central appointment booking A better service will be provided by ensuring compliance with health requirements, especially social distance.</p></div></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-2 kt-pane14_e2b8c8-c7"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title"><strong>How can I get a fingerprint appointment in Meta Kuwait?</strong></span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner"><p>Log in using your credentials at &#8220;Meta Kuwait website&#8221;. On the left, click Appointments. Choose the service you need from a government department or ministry.
